--
-- Table structure for table `comics`
--

CREATE TABLE `comics` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `title` text NOT NULL,
  `time` datetime NOT NULL default '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `published` text NOT NULL,
  `author` text NOT NULL,
  `volume` text NOT NULL,
  `issue` text NOT NULL,
  `rating` text NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=7 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `comments`
--

CREATE TABLE `comments` (
  `type` text NOT NULL,
  `nid` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `poster` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `header` text NOT NULL,
  `message` text NOT NULL,
  `id` int(4) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `time` datetime default NULL,
  `rating` text NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=5782 ;

--
-- Dumping data for table `comments`
--

--
-- Table structure for table `delp_last_searches`
--

  `search_text` text NOT NULL,

  `time` datetime NOT NULL default '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=402 ;

--
-- Table structure for table `files`
--

CREATE TABLE `files` (
  `short_name` text NOT NULL,
  `location` text NOT NULL,
  `submitter` text NOT NULL,
  `category` text NOT NULL,
  `hidden` text NOT NULL,
  `downloads` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `description` text NOT NULL,
  `filetype` text NOT NULL,
  `size` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `local_path` text NOT NULL,
  `time` datetime NOT NULL default '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `thumb` text NOT NULL,
  `worksafe` text NOT NULL,
  `version` text NOT NULL,
  `homepage` text NOT NULL,
  `owner` text NOT NULL,
  `platform` text NOT NULL,
  `os` text NOT NULL,
  `rating` text NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=30 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `games`
--

CREATE TABLE `games` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `poster` text NOT NULL,
  `sname` text NOT NULL,
  `time` datetime NOT NULL default '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `url` text NOT NULL,
  `sfw` text NOT NULL,
  `category` text NOT NULL,
  `rating` text NOT NULL,
  `views` text NOT NULL,
  `hidden` text NOT NULL,
  `bgcolor` text NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=1460 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `link_bin`
--

CREATE TABLE `link_bin` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `link` text NOT NULL,
  `poster` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `time` datetime NOT NULL default '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `bumptime` datetime NOT NULL default '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `sname` text NOT NULL,
  `referrals` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `hidden` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `description` text NOT NULL,
  `clicks` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `rating` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `category` text NOT NULL,
  `friend` text NOT NULL,
  `banned` text NOT NULL,
  `reciprocal` text NOT NULL,
  `referral` text NOT NULL,
  `reviewed` text NOT NULL,
  `interesting` text NOT NULL,
  `adminfav` text NOT NULL,
  `sfw` text NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=204 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `news`
--

CREATE TABLE `news` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `headline` text NOT NULL,
  `message` text NOT NULL,
  `category1` text NOT NULL,
  `category2` text NOT NULL,
  `category3` text NOT NULL,
  `category4` text NOT NULL,
  `submitter` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `time` datetime NOT NULL default '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `image_url` text NOT NULL,
  `image_link` text NOT NULL,
  `image_alt` text NOT NULL,
  `topstory` text NOT NULL,
  `published` text NOT NULL,
  `views` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `rating` text NOT NULL,
  `sfw` text NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 COMMENT='news' AUTO_INCREMENT=236 ;

-- Dumping data for table `news`

INSERT INTO `news` VALUES(233, 'Obvious News Articles', 'There is a trend starting to propagate the internet. News reporters are writing about topics that everyone already knows about. You may have seen what I am talking about firsthand. If you have then that makes this news article obvious to you. That lends credibility to my story. What if this downward spiraling continues? If a majority of people gain knowledge before journalists write their stories, the story becomes obvious.\r\n\r\nLets take a closer look at why journalists might take the \\"obvious\\" approach. First, lets examine the nine elements of journalism, from \\"<a href=http://journalism.org/node/72 target=_blank>The Elements of Journalism</a>\\":\r\n\r\n<p align=center>\r\n<table border=0><tr><td align=left>\r\n1. Journalism\\''s first obligation is to the truth. \r\n2. Its first loyalty is to the citizens. \r\n3. Its essence is discipline of verification. \r\n4. Its practitioners must maintain an independence from those they cover. \r\n5. It must serve as an independent monitor of power. \r\n6. It must provide a forum for public criticism and compromise. \r\n7. It must strive to make the significant interesting, and relevant. \r\n8. It must keep the news comprehensive and proportional. \r\n9. Its practitioners must be allowed to exercise their personal conscience. \r\n</td></tr></table></p>\r\n\r\nIt becomes immediatly clear that when journalists write, they are only reporting the news. They are not adding any opinion or comments that they feel about the story. They are leaving it up to the reader to decide. They write about every concievable thing about what they are writing. They write on all kinds of topics and verify all their sources. They remove themselves from being associated with the story in any way. After the story they ask viewers to provide public feedback and criticism.\r\n\r\n<img src=http://www.defectiveminds.com/images/news/osama.alive.dead.gif align=left> With all that information criteria it becomes even more evident. Journalists are getting lazy. They are starting to spend less time and effort into writing their stories because it is easier to cover something that already is known. There is less risk involved with writing about known things.\r\n\r\nThere may be other reasons why obvious news stories are written. It may be that the writer feels compelled to share the story because he/she feels superior and must \\"inform\\" the ignorant masses. It could be that even though everyone DOES know about the story, the writer thinks that by writing it, it will get people to think more critically about the topic.\r\n\r\nHowever, obviousness is subjective. Let\\''s say that someone wrote something that everyone knew. Everyone from our planet that is. Aliens from outer space would not know (unless they had been monitoring). People from remote and strange places such as Florida would have no idea.\r\n\r\nSome people watch something and it becomes obvious the next time they watch it. Like if you watch something on television and then someone comes in the room and they just see it because the news channel likes to repeat the story every 5 minutes. The person joining you is all like, \\"Wow that happened?\\" So you go, \\"Phshaw... You didn\\''t know?\\" like you are a subject matter expert on the news story.\r\n\r\nAll of this information about journalism obviousness leads me to believe something. If journalism is obvious then it is obvious the journalists are doing their jobs.\r\n\r\nSee also: <a href=http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ric_Romero target=_blank>Ric Romero</a>, <a href=http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Journalism target=_blank>Journalism</a>\r\n', 'Obvious', '', '', '', 1, '2008-01-13 11:13:17', 'http://www.defectiveminds.com/images/news/romero.jpg', '', '', 'no', 'yes', 63, '', '');

--
-- Table structure for table `photoshopper`
--

CREATE TABLE `photoshopper` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `message` text NOT NULL,
  `user` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `image_url` text NOT NULL,
  `image_localpath` text NOT NULL,
  `image_alt` text NOT NULL,
  `time` datetime NOT NULL default '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `category` text NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=4 ;

--
-- Table structure for table `poll_data`
--

CREATE TABLE `poll_data` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `Option1` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `Option2` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `Option3` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `Votes` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `Title` text NOT NULL,
  `Question` text NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`ID`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=2 ;
